" investing enough meet future energy needs, uncertainties setting stage volatile period ahead," said IEA chief Fatih Birol.
PARIS: global transition clean energy still far too slow meet climate pledges risks fuelling even greater price volatility, International Energy Agency warned Wednesday.
" investing enough meet future energy needs, uncertainties setting stage volatile period ahead," said IEA chief Fatih Birol.
" social economic benefits accelerating clean energy transitions huge, costs inaction immense."
annual World Energy Outlook report -- published just weeks before COP26 summit Glasgow -- IEA calculated investment clean energy projects infrastructure need trebled decade if those pledges met.
At summit, countries come pressure commit decisive action limit global warming 1.5 degrees Celsius above pre-industrial levels, pledged landmark 2015 Paris climate agreement.
IEA -- advises developed countries energy policy -- said renewables wind solar energy continued grow rapidly, electric vehicles set new sales records 2020, even economies bent weight Covid-19 lockdowns.

However, " clean energy progress still far too slow put global emissions sustained decline net zero" 2050, agency believes help limit increase global temperatures 1.5C.
agency analysed possible scenarios.
looked measures governments put place specific policies actively developing.
And almost increased energy demand until 2050 met low emissions sources, annual emissions still roughly same today developing economies build nationwide infrastructure, IEA said.
Under scenario, temperatures 2100 2.6C higher pre-industrial levels.
second scenario looked promises made some governments achieve net-zero emissions future, see doubling clean energy investment financing decade.
If pledges fully implemented time, demand fossil fuels peak 2025, global CO2 emissions fall 40 percent 2050, IEA said.
Here, global average temperature increase 2100 2.1C, represent improvement, still way above 1.5C agreed Paris accord, concluded.
"Reaching path requires investment clean energy projects infrastructure triple decade," Birol said.
"Some 70 percent additional spending needs happen emerging developing economies."
IEA argued extra investment might less burden some might think.
"More 40 percent required emissions reductions come measures pay themselves, improving efficiency, limiting gas leakage, installing wind solar places competitive electricity generation technologies," said.
report highlighted insufficient investment contributing uncertainty future.
"Spending oil natural gas depressed price collapses 2014-15 again 2020. result, geared world stagnant even falling demand," IEA said.
"At same time, spending clean energy transitions far below what required meet future needs sustainable way."
means energy markets face "bumpy ride" if investment renewables increased, IEA said.
#3
Several Tamil Nadu' industries both energy intensive customer price sensitive, particularly precarious current time energy prices soaring highly volatile globally. Energy efficiency innovation renewable process heating cooling therefore critical business continuity growth whilst necessary mitigating greenhouse gas emissions contribute climate change.
Investing sustainable industrial energy transition makes good business sense, demonstrated United Nations Industrial Development Organization (UNIDO) partners Tamil Nadu elsewhere.
Coimbatore home flourishing foundry industry serving pumps, automotive, machine, textile engineering industries. Energy costs account average 30%-35% manufacturing costs foundries, melting section consuming lion' share nearly 70%. Foundries typically save 5%-10% energy bill -established energy efficiency techniques better operating practices. UNIDO Bureau Energy Efficiency (BEE) Coimbatore Industrial Infrastructure Association (COINDIA) supported implementation energy efficiency micro, small medium foundries Coimbatore region. At least 130 foundries implemented 253 measures cumulative investment Rs30 crore. resulted energy savings nearly 1,600 tonnes oil equivalent, reduced greenhouse gas emissions 15,500 tonnes achieved annual cost savings Rs23 crore.
project documented 21 specific techniques eight typically require investment less Rs2 lakh, seven require investment Rs10 lakh remaining six need Rs10 lakh investment. One foundry invested Rs44 lakh replace conventional cupola furnace energy efficient 12 pulse induction furnace payback 1.6. Another firm installed efficient shot blast machine Rs8.9 lakh simple pay back 3.7. replacement old motor energy efficient IE3 motor achieved another foundry pay back 1.4 initial investment Rs2.8 lakh. addition variable frequency drive existing screw compressor cost Rs2.9 lakh achieved payback eight months. Some foundries went renewable energy, foundry setting 1MWh solar plant cost Rs495 lakh expected pay back 3.2.
COINDA acquired energy monitoring instruments project conduct energy audits foundry sectors. Up 50% state-level subsidies available conducting energy efficiency audit 25% grant investment recommended energy efficiency measures.
Vellore home vibrant rice milling cluster. collaboration ministry MSME, UNIDO partners zooming replicable energy efficiency solutions standardise bulk procure, finance future energy costs savings energy service contracts Energy Efficiency Services Limited. So far, technologies successfully demonstrated. innovative LSU dryer system investment Rs12 lakh saves 15% fuel 65% power delivers uniform dried grain leading lower milling losses, thereby achieving pay back less. Replacement traditional boilers energy efficient boilers investment Rs60 lakh saves Rs23 lakh annual fuel costs.

Energy efficiency goes hand hand clean-tech innovation, UNIDO works BEE Facility Low Carbon Technology Deployment (FLCTD). Annual innovation challenges organised covering six technology domains: space conditioning, waste heat recovery, pumping, electric energy storage, industrial Internet Things (IoT) industrial resource efficiency. Winning innovators supported technical advice, industry demonstration sites partial grant funding deploy validate innovations. So far 59 innovators selected 559 applications, receiving Rs18 crore financial support. 18 innovations completed independent validation twelve thereof commercialized.
Renewable energy integral part industrial energy transition. Most efforts focused renewable power generation solar wind energy. Many industries do require thermal energy low medium temperatures, achieved solar thermal systems. With UNIDO' support Natural Capsules Limited Puducherry installed 64 parabolic dish collectors each measuring 4.4sqm produce hot water 105C production. system saves 150 liters diesel day, enables company recover investment technology three--half. Ranipet Tannery Effluent Treatment company installing system crossed compound parabolic concentrators total areas 1,590 square meters generate 1.5 ton steam hour project cost 353 lakh.
Energy efficiency achieved productivity measures reduce rejects minimise rework. Energy efficiency indeed integral part manufacturing excellence aimed eliminating wastages manufacturing, Swachh Udyog. involves efficiency using energy, material water, effectiveness terms meeting customer requirements maturity monitoring predictive control manufacturing processes.
post pandemic industrial development scenario shaped few global trends, reorganisation global value chains, digitalisation manufacturing, Industry 4.0, transition low carbon circular economy. These present growth diversification opportunity India, provided manufacturing compete internationally. Energy intensive sectors foundries, textile food processing choice pursuing energy efficiency, clean-tech innovation renewable energy process heating cooling.

How do you define energy equity?
There dimensions. inequality within energy systems, manifest underprivileged don't access energy electricity. Then, worldwide level, global energy inequality wealthier countries consuming energy capita absolute terms poorer countries.
Energy vital raising standards living enhancing development. critical building saving lives - situations intense heat, instance, access air cooling systems imperative. Energy access necessary improve worker productivity. Inequality energy access undermines economic activity efforts raise poverty. Energy inequality translates lower living standards hurt poor deeply. There situations poor spend incomes energy affluent families - times, poor spend unit energy wealthier. example, energy delivered grid less expensive using batteries power appliances - latter shows absolute energy inequality. Poor often older vehicles less fuel- efficient. So, fuel travel same distance others. These just some ways poor spend energy can't save invest important areas. Energy inequity traps them cycle poverty.
Has pandemic highlighted energy poverty?
pandemic brought fore how poor suffer impacts crisis due lack access energy., poorer communities suffered because employment conditions exposed them virus. poor couldn't stay home, working computers remotely. Lacking energy access, go earn livelihoods. many countries, poor received inadequate healthcare, weakened lack quality energy reflected power outages, etc. pandemic showed how inequality actually kill energy large factor impacting peoples' access life-saving services
A BUNDLE OF INEQUITIES: Energy inequality reflected dependence unclean fuels severe health impacts impoverish vulnerable
Where does India stand energy equity?
India huge importance terms energy landscape. India' robust economic growth 15. future, India likely join, China, Germany Japan top five economies world. India projected largest energy demand globally. So, what happens India very important terms global energy system efforts decarbonise. But, alongside, poor India particularly vulnerable terms energy poverty compared poor affluent societies. So, it' even important plan greater energy access. issue energy equity empowering poorer nations get clean, sustainable energy help them grow exists global level - India very good advocate. But must remember energy equity marginalised communities within national context.

Can energy poverty reduced world aims decreasing emissions?
One world' greatest challenges reduce energy poverty supporting economic growth. It' important prioritise basic energy access, electricity cooking technologies, etc., extremely poor. Alongside, developing countries need broaden energy access businesses middle class. What climate situation does reduce some options. Clearly, need transition lower carbon energy.
India, largest projected energy demand globally, must plan transition rapidly possible securing ability generate electricity near future. Advanced economies should help India achieve - context COP26, world' richest countries should step financing help developing nations transition lower carbon economy meeting development needs.
How energy transition made equitable fair those facing energy poverty?
question values priorities - means recognising importance growth transition dynamic benefits. Globally, energy efforts often serve interests elite,
disenfranchised. Countries give lip service issue isn't followed much. Media coverage important highlight energy gap keep focus efforts solve. helps raising public consciousness lead issue becoming part dialogue. It' notable India made concerted effort provide hundreds millions access electricity. Now, it' important engage energy marginalised understand needs. A study India found less electricity theft occurs when communities enjoy trusting relationship local electricity company. So, simple changes attitudes bring better impacts, better bottom lines energy producers.



Is energy equity core world' transition sustainable energy?
Energy equity paramount right type energy transition. don't want world powered renewables energy poverty still impacts poor harshly. don't need energy transition terms emissions technologies - need right type energy transition empower millions. Energy equity central.

#16
For time, bottom- 'Just Energy Transition Framework' formulated researchers IIT-Kanpur, recently published peer-reviewed international journal Sustainability. Taking account climate crises-induced 'energy transition' (ET) process India, research attempts develop framework community-centric local governments (LG) play pivotal roles ensure energy justice (EJ) thousands might lose livelihoods process.
India' dependence coal primary energy supply may ignored near future, coal set see slow growth 30% whereas solar energy likely observe massive surge 700% 2030.
If India aims phase coal mining 2050 15-20 million livelihoods likely affected. To ensure EJ process mine closure installing new solar plants, decentralised local governance extremely relevant, paper said.
paper presents bottom- inverted pyramid framework 'Just Energy Transition' (JET) consisting four layers., coal mine workers local residents top ' vulnerable sections' consequently, biggest stakeholders. Immediately below local government. Both coal mine workers local government should interact civil bodies (trade unions, NGOs, research organisations) negotiating transitions state (provincial) government national (federal) government, bottom framework, said paper.
LG mechanism function nodal point disbursement national state welfare policy programmes, bottom pyramid engages communities policy formulation, implementation, monitoring. JET fits community-centric LG strengthens decentralisation decision-making process. Centralising JET (top-down approach), hand, weaken community sensitivity response.
"Justice prevail if everyone involved decision-making policy implementation process," said research paper titled Local Government Just Energy Transition: Towards Community-Centric Framework.
"Inter LG alliance stakeholders [miners], scientists, workers, business groups, policymakers, individuals energy supply chain play crucial role govern transition effectively. However, alliance must tune national policies. While demand funds services meet energy need flow down stakeholders national government, flow funds regulatory policy move national government stakeholders." said
Pradip Swarnakar, lead author paper Professor sociology heads Just Transition Research Centre (JTRC) IIT Kanpur.
article finds global absence conceptual framework locate JET within realm LG fills wide gap knowledge relation JET processes outcome local level. success model, paper says, lies identifying key local stakeholders trade unions workers strengthening institutions decentralise JET LG system.
Key findings:
� Energy justice governance gained currency post-Paris agreement period (2016-2022)
� A small number scientific works indicates dearth research focussing EJ ET local level
� Complex relations technology society necessitated paradigm shift mere ET just energy transition (JET)
� Development JET just started infusing policy interventions global South (Canada, Europe, USA, Australia), groundwork LG ET begun Global North (Asia Africa).
� Centralised JET weakens community' sensitivity response; decentralised decision-making, essential step localising JET
� Four vital conceptual pillars EJ - distributive (access resources ), procedural (participation decision-making process), cosmopolitan (human rights governed moral values), recognition (vulnerability due socioeconomic status)
� Strengthening LG systems giving budgetary support key successful transition, helps minimise conflict business firms facilitates stakeholders' participation multilevel governing mechanisms
� From installing large solar grids establishing energy parks building small storage devices, input science technology pivotal. Low-cost consumer-friendly technology preferred, challenge absorbing left-behind fossil fuel workers clear.
� Heavy investment solution seems affordable global north; global south afford capital-intensive plans. Therefore, need alternative low-cost yet community-centric governance mechanism JET.

#42
What core your research?
I am historian energy, environment economics. I'm broadly interested relationships human societies energy systems how modern energy systems fuelled types economic growth never seen before Earth. I focus how systems made sustainable long-term thriving future.
You write America' unprecedented turn fossil fuels early 20th century - what drove?
I'd emphasise role transport systems here. When I studied USA' fossil fuel transition, what stood how far places derived energy ended using. Secondly, wasn't simple mine drill, real struggle building ways moving energy reliable scalable steps consumers lived - came down canals pipelines shipped oil wires transmitted electricity. Understanding energy systems looks different when you put those transport networks front.
You write energy' benefits very unequal - why?
Inequality endemic fossil fuel regime - goes back power extracted gets used. regions produce energy benefit far less places consume. big cities eastern seaboard grew tremendously era fossil fuel expansion - New York, Philadelphia Baltimore boomed, many profitable industries benefitting. But rural areas bore very real costs mining, industrial accidents health impacts. Bringing coal oil underground leached toxic minerals water supplies damaged lands. These face much costs energy systems consumers far away.
You chronicle America' energy transition marked 'fraud, failure frustration' - why so?
I trying capture how early transition fossil fuels, remarkably hard get consumers even want - I think analogy today when still early stages renewable energy transition. When coal oil emerged, quite uncertain them - very unsure having constantly running electricity walls houses. took long time convince safe. Certain coals wouldn't burn some opened fire. Switching woodfire coal meant getting costly stoves abandoning pleasant smell light wood offered. Similarly, oil, used lanterns, often poorly refined exploded. At start, energy transitions obvious seem retrospect - work convince consumers try them.
I wrote 'fraud' apropos America' coal transition happened anthracite coal very hard burn. It' above 90% carbon - light, you need very hot fire air go particular way. Since consumers didn't know how do, some coal merchants accused fraudsters selling useless black stone.
imagine energy abstract - what does 'materiality' mean?
Before fossil fuels, almost energy came plants, those grew feed ourselves, animals - then used labour - trees burnt heat cooking. Energy mostly local - you grew near you. So, people' connection very different.
With materiality fossil fuel systems, absolutely enormous networks behind scenes when press switch refuel car. modern world designed making energy easy access - energy seems 'invisible' when you've built huge systems pipes, wires terminals landscapes. Energy seem abstract when those using don't see consequences producing - lighting homes New York aren't seeing West Virginia mountains cleared coal.
what does your term 'petromyopia' mean?
Many analysts equate energy oil - much 20th century, oil arguably attractive energy source. It' dramatic, tied geopolitics appears cultural forms movies. Yet, I've found oil never 35% global energy consumption. Human societies many energy sources just foundational how live, work play - petromyopia hides ways coal, natural gas, biomass, animal power human labour essential parts energy systems.

How just transition different energy transition?
Climate change experienced different parts globe learnt much triggered greenhouse gases. If want contain global warming within 1.5�C range, must act cutting down emissions. To achieve target, some countries must phase fossil fuels, coal, others must phase down. phase down coal simply energy transition because mainstay economy many states country century. While switching renewable energy sources, must think engaged sector socio-economic political impacts transition. moment keep 'people' discussions energy transition, must equitable sustainable so minimal adverse masses. process described term 'just' basically means 'injustice' anyone.
Why talking just transition when energy transition does seem reality Jharkhand? Alongside talks coal phase-down, nod given new coal mines every second day state.

When talk coal phase down phase achieve net-zero target 2070, talking states individually. goal country some states may positive side some negative side., coal cheap abundant, infrastructure, developed coal energy source. take time overhaul entire ecosystem till then, need coal. Though question better answered policy makers, what understand achieving net-zero goal long-drawn process even if new mines come, closure others demand fossil fuel come down gradually. Every state must prepared scenario if Jharkhand taking lead becoming future-ready, nothing wrong.

What role UNDP playing realising goal net zero just transition?
UNDP supporting agent help various govts meet targets. ask uncomfortable questions help them achieve goals keeping society considerations. partnered task force just transition ( govt Jharkhand). Through National Livelihood Mission, ensure generation livelihood scopes areas affected climate change. arrange funds carrying projects, ensure money reaches right hands assist capacity-building. Bihar, distributed solar cold storage facilities 'Jeevika didis' (women SHGs state govt' rural development department) so litchi stored sold market minimum wastage. Jharkhand, assisting brainstorming engaging partners globe conferences, so road map prepared.
There SoPs mine closure reclaiming land closed mines hardly followed. Do you think linking finances compliance reports solution?
I don't believe punitive action though carrot--stick approach taken better results. analyse reasons poor implementation guidelines case mine closure. Say, example, if alternative job opportunities local populace, still take illegal mining activities even after mine closures. see underlying reason then decide. Sometimes, incentivizing right practices brings better results.
Jharkhand coal-rich state when see renewable infrastructure, developed western southern states country. Is beginning "unjust" transition?
Energy security come any state I said energy transition must ensure just transition. explore new industries, suiting area accordingly skill them ready. Maybe some agriculture practice some sort cottage industry help engage. part discussions UNDP holds various levels so do suffer livelihood front, local needs demands should taken consideration.

India finds itself crossroads wrestles complexities meeting escalating energy demands striving transition cleaner, renewable sources. Recent research indicates nation' energy subsidies surged nine- high, reaching INR 3.2 lakh crore (USD 39.3 billion) fiscal ending 2023.
Despite positioning itself global climate leader recent, India' reliance fossil fuels remains significant, coal, oil, gas subsidies contributing approximately 40% total energy subsidies FY 2023.
stands stark contrast clean energy subsidies, accounted less 10% total.
surge fossil fuel subsidies attributed part 2022 global energy crisis, exacerbated Russia' invasion Ukraine, prompting India implement measures stabilize domestic energy prices. These measures included capping retail prices petrol, diesel, liquefied petroleum gas, providing tax cuts direct transfers businesses consumers.
According report International Institute Sustainable Development (IISD), oil gas subsidies alone rose 63% FY 2023 compared previous fiscal. Similarly, coal subsidies increased 17% same period, reflecting India' continued dependence fossil fuels despite ambitions clean energy transition.
With rapid economic growth propelling India USD 5 trillion economy 2027, government investing heavily forms energy supply. However, experts caution approach hinder progress India' clean energy goals 2030 perpetuate dependence volatile geopolitically risky fossil fuels.
Swasti Raizada, Policy Advisor IISD, emphasized need targeted subsidies return market- pricing avoid mounting budgetary impacts. Raizada stressed untargeted fossil fuel subsidies inefficient detract fiscal resources available supporting clean energy technologies.

light challenges, report recommends government consider reallocating portion fossil fuel tax revenues support just transition cleaner energy sources. Deepak Sharma, Policy Analyst IISD, underscored importance ensuring state-owned enterprises align India' net-zero commitments facilitate sustainable inclusive energy transition.
India clearly grapples dual imperatives meeting rising energy demands reducing carbon emissions. path forward hinges decisive policy actions prioritize clean energy investments mitigating adverse impacts fossil fuel subsidies.

#142
India, burgeoning population rapidly expanding urbanization, faces pressing need address environmental concerns reduce carbon footprint - specifically transportation sector number trucks required quadruple 2050. Since COP28 aimed addressing critical intersection climate change global health, emphasis need swift substantial reductions greenhouse gas emissions meet zero emissions target 2070.
country strives sustainable development, spotlight transitioning transportation sector clean energy intensified. Thus, clarion call switch cleaner fuels transportation logistics sector.
Switching Clean Trucking
With rapid growth demand road freight, decarbonisation heavy trucking segment become even important. India, medium- heavy-duty trucking sector constitutes mere 4% total vehicle population. Yet, responsible 40% overall road transportation emissions - surpassing vehicle segments primarily because elevated fuel consumption. India realized logistics carbon footprint thus undertaking endeavours transform logistics landscape achieve clean trucking. government emphasizing decarbonization transportation sector facilitating adoption eco-friendly modes LNG trucks, electric vehicles, flexible-fuel vehicles hydrogen-powered fuel cell electric vehicles (FCEVs).
From long haul transportation perspective: LNG (liquefied natural gas) cleaner-burning fuel produces lower emissions compared diesel, making attractive option reducing environmental. LNG trucks present compelling alternative heavy duty long-haul transportation, superior Total Cost Ownership (TCO) range coupled unmatched reliability. Designed successful natural gas engine, delivering impressive torque horsepower, trucks prioritize fuel efficiency quieter operations compared diesel engines. Since fuel available condense form trucks feature suitable cryogenic fuel tank, cover significant distances 1000 kms single fill, alleviating range anxiety concerns. integration advanced telematics systems ensures secure journeys, expanding LNG dispensing network promises comprehensive coverage major routes, reducing need frequent refills. summary, LNG trucks redefine efficiency sustainability realm long-haul transportation.
For short hauls: Advancements battery technology, particularly cost reductions, increased energy density, possible electrify trucks, prospect once deemed remote. When widely implemented, battery electric trucks offer lower total cost ownership compared diesel counterparts various weight categories. Additionally, electric trucks powered renewable domestically produced energy replace diesel trucks. addition economic benefits, transition battery electric trucks promises improved environmental advantages, potential greenhouse gas intensity reductions ranging 9% 35% different truck classes compared diesel, considering India' current average grid emissions intensity.
How Large Corporations Leading Change
shift near zero-emission trucks India necessitates proactive involvement consumers, investors, corporate entities. Businesses India aiming reduce indirect emissions capitalizing freight electrification, particularly key trucking segments parcels consumer goods deliveries (approximately 45% trucks) perishables ( 18%). Major freight users, particularly those utilizing third-party logistics providers, influence drive transition electric trucks.
Recognizing importance sustainability, India' Fortune 500 companies CONCOR, Dalmia Cement, JSW Steel, JK Laxmi Cement, UltraTech Cement, Tata Steel, Reliance, Nestle, others, leading charge embracing LNG trucks inbound logistics raw material movement. Hence, industry leaders making significant strides adopting cleaner efficient transportation options.
Original equipment manufacturers (OEMs) collaborating international leaders alternate fuel green trucks accelerate progress production diverse green truck models. swift development ecosystem infrastructure, supply service networks, LNG pumps, charging points, etc. holds paramount significance transporters considering transition green trucks. Notably, key industry players Oil Marketing Companies (OMCs), GAIL, subsidiaries, Bharat Liquefied Natural Gas (BLNG) actively establishing 50-70 LNG retail outlets nationwide, currently 9 functional. Similar initiatives taken establishing charging infrastructure EV vehicles. These initiatives seeking governmental support facilitate rapid transition cleaner fuels.
Way Forward
Strategic partnerships supply chain vital sustainable future India' trucking industry. collective efforts government, truck manufacturers alternate fuel providers battery manufacturers, & oil marketing companies, key corporates fleet operators, charging infrastructure providers instrumental establishing thriving market clean trucks. Strengthening collaborations catalyse widespread deployment green trucks throughout country. India embarks journey toward decarbonization, success efforts embracing clean trucking hinges collaborative efforts shared commitment innovation sustainability. By fostering partnerships encouraging increased public-private cooperation, adhere COP26 commitment pave way greener, healthier, prosperous future.

Early election results show Donald Trump potentially taking early lead Kamala Harris, political analysts caution against premature victory declarations. Vote-counting processes, particularly battleground states, shift initial results mail- absentee ballots tallied days following election night.

Early trends suggest former President Republican nominee Donald Trump secured initial lead approximately 150 electoral votes vice president Kamala Harris. However, political analysts warn early advantage may reveal ultimate outcome, Democratic candidate Kamala Harris still reverse tide.
phenomenon, often dubbed "mirages" elections, set play central role shaping public perceptions election night, especially battleground states vote-counting quirks paint misleading pictures.
What gave Trump chance claim 'stolen election'
2020, states Pennsylvania Wisconsin exhibited what experts call "red mirage," showing Trump leading election night before "blue shift" occurred mail- ballots heavily favored Democrats tallied, ultimately pushing Joe Biden lead.
Trump' team utilized pattern push claims stolen election, though outcome merely consequence state' voting laws mail- ballot trends. week, similar dynamics expected, see shift -person votes counted states North Carolina Georgia.

Why declaring victory complex
ballots roll, Trump' campaign reportedly plans declare victory should appear cross critical 270 electoral vote mark- move experts say premature given complexities ballot processing various states.

With large portion Democratic voters populous urban areas, vote processing tends slower, delayed counts heavily influence final tallies days following Election Day. variance vote reporting leave some states, particularly Pennsylvania Arizona, caught prolonged counting process absentee ballots trickle.
What delays results
Each battleground state own timeline rules processing votes, perceived winner election night. Pennsylvania, instance, prohibits election officials counting mail- ballots until morning Election Day, potentially delaying results days Democratic mail- votes gradually reduce Trump' -person voting advantage. A new law aims ease concerns requiring counties disclose number outstanding mail ballots midnight, helping preempt misinformation.
Wisconsin, votes processed centrally major cities, large early-morning dumps absentee ballots may again tip scales Harris' favor, just did Biden 2020. Similarly, North Carolina, known extended vote canvassing, may keep Americans guessing days absentee overseas ballots continue counted even after election night.
states Arizona, voting mail highly popular, early results show Harris lead due early mail- ballots, though numbers might edge Trump -person votes. trend may reverse again once mail ballots- those dropped off Election Day- counted subsequent days.
Nevada, infamous protracted counting process 2020, see swifter tabulation due new regulations allowing early ballot processing weeks before Election Day. However, Nevada' allowance late-arriving mail ballots postmarked November 5 may delay final result, historically Democratic late ballots counted.

India' leading companies lagging renewable energy goals, Climate Risk Horizon reports
India' top companies, particularly heavy industries steel, cement, textiles, lagging behind meeting renewable energy decarbonisation goals, according Climate Risk Horizons. Despite ambitious commitments, 5% electricity consumption comes renewables. Strengthened regulatory efforts deemed essential close gap promote energy security.
India' leading companies falling short meeting nation' ambitious renewable energy decarbonisation targets, according new analysis think tank Climate Risk Horizons (CRH). industrial sector, accounts half India' energy consumption, plays critical role government' decarbonisation efforts.
report titled "Slow Switch," CRH evaluated 33 companies seven industries.
Five industries major energy consumers-Cement, Steel, Aluminium, Textiles, Fertilisers- Information Technology Fast-Moving Consumer Goods (FMCG). Using publicly available data annual sustainability reports, analysis assessed companies' decarbonisation progress FY 2023.
findings reveal significant gap companies' renewable energy commitments actual actions. Only 5% annual electricity consumption assessed companies comes renewable sources solar wind. Except ArcelorMittal/Nippon Steel, companies reported energy consumption various sources. Despite ambitious commitments members global renewable energy alliances, nearly off track meet goals. Notable examples include:
* Steel Industry: Companies JSW, Jindal, Tata Steel, ArcelorMittal/Nippon Steel sourcing less 0.05% energy renewables average.
* Textile Industry: Firms Trident, Welspun, Arvind, Shahi aligned targets Paris Agreement, less 3% energy consumption renewable sources.
* Cement Industry: Major players Ultratech, ACC, Ambuja aim reduce emissions Paris Agreement, yet renewables account 2.5% energy.
* FMCG Sector: Companies Godrej, ITC, Britannia low renewable energy utilisation, contrasting better performers Nestle Hindustan Unilever.
information technology sector emerged top performer overall, fertiliser industry received lowest scores.
"Shifting renewable energy essential energy security both company national levels. While few large companies started move direction, much needs done quickly if India meet decarbonisation targets," said Vishnu Teja, lead author report.
India' regulations mandate large electricity consumers must source 30% electricity renewable sources, yet companies analysed average 5% renewable electricity consumption. report underscores heavy industry sector' potential drive decarbonisation India' electricity system. These companies' annual electricity consumption exceeds 169 billion units, double states Andhra Pradesh West Bengal, yet less 5% sourced renewables.
Strengthening enforcing renewable purchase obligations crucial developing renewable energy capacity energy storage technologies, lower costs enhance energy security industries economy.
"India Inc needs step invest energy-secure future. country' renewable energy decarbonisation targets met active support large corporate players. With green energy open access regulations place, companies should signing Power Purchase Agreements ensure 100% electricity comes renewable sources 2030," said Ashish Fernandes, CEO Climate Risk Horizons -author report.

Researchers IIT Guwahati developed cost-efficient, high-performance photodetector using formamidinium perovskite plasmonic nanoparticles. innovation, published *ACS Applied Materials & Interfaces*, enhances light absorption sensitivity, making ideal applications healthcare, environmental monitoring, solar energy.
Researchers Indian Institute Technology (IIT) Guwahati developed advanced, cost-efficient photodetector potential revolutionize industries healthcare, environmental monitoring, solar energy. cutting-edge device unique combination formamidinium perovskite plasmonic nanoparticles, making highly sensitive light remaining affordable durable.Photodetectors, essential devices modern technology, detect light convert electrical signals. They integral various applications, cameras, medical imaging equipment, environmental sensors, communication systems. Despite importance, achieving high-performance photodetectors low production cost long challenge. team IIT Guwahati made significant breakthrough addressing challenge. research, published respected *ACS Applied Materials & Interfaces* journal, led Prof. P. K. Giri IIT Guwahati' Department Physics, contributions his research scholars, Debabrata Sahu, Subhankar Debnath, Sirsendu Ghosal. team focused using perovskite materials-known superior light absorption properties- commonly applied solar cells light-sensitive technologies. particular, formamidinium- perovskite chosen study offers high stability efficient light--electricity conversion. However, balancing light absorption efficiency affordability persistent issue.
To enhance performance photodetector, IIT Guwahati researchers incorporated array 2D-printed plasmonic nanoparticles. These nanoparticles, composed silver (Ag), designed concentrate light onto perovskite layer via phenomenon known localized surface plasmon resonance (LSPR). LSPR allows effective focusing light, significantly boosts light absorption improves photodetector' performance.Prof. P. K. Giri explained, "Our aim create photodetector combines efficiency, affordability, durability, making suitable real-world applications. By integrating 2D-printed plasmonic nanoparticles, notably enhanced device' performance made production process both scalable cost-effective." team achieved improvement employing precise microprinting technique arrange silver nanoparticles. technique enhances device' sensitivity keeping manufacturing process economical. resulting photodetector remains stable typical environmental conditions, ensuring suitability practical multiple sectors. innovative photodetector technology holds promise multiple applications. healthcare, improve accuracy quality medical imaging, aiding earlier accurate diagnoses. For environmental monitoring, enhanced sensitivity lead precise detection pollutants harmful substances. Additionally, solar energy industry, improved light absorption capabilities photodetector contribute efficient energy conversion, supporting renewable energy goals. IIT Guwahati team' breakthrough paves way broader adoption advanced photodetectors various industries reducing costs enhancing performance. Their work addresses significant technological challenges contributes solutions global issues related health, environmental protection, sustainable energy. development promising step forward making high-quality photodetection technology accessible impactful real-world applications.

Renewable energy: Sustainable Alternative
Renewable energy sources, solar, wind, hydropower, gained significant momentum recent. They provide cleaner sustainable alternative fossil fuels, main source greenhouse gas emissions. According International Renewable Energy Agency (IREA), renewable energy accounted 72 percent global electricity capacity additions 2019. remarkable growth demonstrates increasing recognition crucial role renewable energy mitigating climate change.
Smart grids
addition renewable energy, smart grids gained traction crucial tool combating climate change. Smart grids modern electricity networks leverage advanced technologies optimise electricity generation, distribution, consumption. They enable better integration renewable energy sources, enhance energy efficiency facilitate energy storage technologies. Smart grids empower consumers providing them real-time data energy usage, allowing them informed decisions energy consumption. By enabling efficient, resilient flexible electricity system, smart grids driving transition sustainable energy future.
Carbon capture
Carbon capture utilisation (CCU) technologies another innovative solution fight against climate change. CCU involves capturing carbon dioxide (CO2) emissions industrial processes utilising them produce valuable products store them permanently. technology potential significantly reduce CO2 emissions industries cement, steel, chemicals, major contributors greenhouse gas emissions. CCU helps reducing emissions provides economic opportunities creating new markets carbon- products, building materials fuels.
Sustainable agriculture
Sustainable agriculture vital area technology play significant role mitigating climate change. Agricultural practices, deforestation, intensive farming, excessive fertilizers, contribute greenhouse gas emissions environmental degradation. However, innovative technologies precision farming, hydroponics, vertical farming revolutionizing agriculture reducing water usage, optimizing resource utilization, reducing greenhouse gas emissions. These technologies making agriculture sustainable improving food security nutrition communities world.
It' imperative recognize innovative technologies standalone solutions rather interconnected pieces larger puzzle. By combining renewable energy, smart grids, carbon capture, sustainable agriculture, create synergistic effect maximises climate change. For instance, renewable energy power production hydrogen electrolysis, then utilized clean sustainable fuel various industries. Additionally, smart grids optimize integration renewable energy utilization hydrogen, enabling efficient flexible energy system.
However, realizing full potential technologies requires collective effort stakeholders, governments, businesses, communities. Governments must create supportive policies, regulations, incentives promote development adoption technologies.
